/usr/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba src/spawn.ts | sed -n '1,240p'" in /home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	import type { EvolverDetection, EvolverSpawnOptions, EvolverSpawnResult } from "./types.ts";
     2	
     3	let cachedDetection: EvolverDetection | null = null;
     4	let detectionAttempted = false;
     5	
     6	export async function detectEvolver(): Promise<EvolverDetection | null> {
     7		if (detectionAttempted) {
     8			return cachedDetection;
     9		}
    10		detectionAttempted = true;
    11	
    12		try {
    13			const whichProc = Bun.spawn(["which", "evolver"], {
    14				stdout: "pipe",
    15				stderr: "pipe",
    16			});
    17			const whichExit = await whichProc.exited;
    18			if (whichExit !== 0) {
    19				return null;
    20			}
    21			const binaryPath = (await new Response(whichProc.stdout).text()).trim();
    22	
    23			let version = "unknown";
    24			try {
    25				const proc = Bun.spawn(["evolver"], {
    26					stdout: "pipe",
    27					stderr: "pipe",
    28				});
    29				await proc.exited;
    30				const output = await new Response(proc.stdout).text();
    31				const match = output.match(/(\d+\.\d+\.\d+)/);
    32				if (match && match[1]) {
    33					version = match[1];
    34				}
    35			} catch {
    36				// version extraction failure is non-fatal
    37			}
    38	
    39			cachedDetection = { path: binaryPath, version };
    40			return cachedDetection;
    41		} catch (error) {
    42			console.warn("[EvoMapBridge/spawn] evolver detection failed", error);
    43			return null;
    44		}
    45	}
    46	
    47	export async function spawnEvolver(options: EvolverSpawnOptions): Promise<EvolverSpawnResult> {
    48		const {
    49			command,
    50			args = [],
    51			stdin,
    52			cwd,
    53			timeoutMs = 5000,
    54			env,
    55		} = options;
    56	
    57		const procArgs = [command, ...args];
    58	
    59		try {
    60			const proc = Bun.spawn(["evolver", ...procArgs], {
    61				stdout: "pipe",
    62				stderr: "pipe",
    63				stdin: stdin ? "pipe" : undefined,
    64				cwd,
    65				env: env ? { ...process.env, ...env } : process.env,
    66			});
    67	
    68			if (stdin && proc.stdin) {
    69				proc.stdin.write(new TextEncoder().encode(stdin));
    70				proc.stdin.end();
    71			}
    72	
    73			const timeoutPromise = new Promise<"timeout">((resolve) => {
    74				setTimeout(() => resolve("timeout"), timeoutMs);
    75			});
    76	
    77			const result = await Promise.race([
    78				(async () => {
    79					const exitCode = await proc.exited;
    80					const stdout = await new Response(proc.stdout).text();
    81					const stderr = await new Response(proc.stderr).text();
    82					return { stdout, stderr, exitCode, timedOut: false } as EvolverSpawnResult;
    83				})(),
    84				timeoutPromise,
    85			]);
    86	
    87			if (result === "timeout") {
    88				proc.kill();
    89				const stdout = await new Response(proc.stdout).text().catch(() => "");
    90				const stderr = await new Response(proc.stderr).text().catch(() => "");
    91				return {
    92					stdout,
    93					stderr,
    94					exitCode: null,
    95					timedOut: true,
    96				};
    97			}
    98	
    99			return result;
   100		} catch (error) {
   101			return {
   102				stdout: "",
   103				stderr: String(error),
   104				exitCode: null,
   105				timedOut: false,
   106			};
   107		}
   108	}
   109	
   110	export async function isEvolverAvailable(): Promise<boolean> {
   111		const detection = await detectEvolver();
   112		return detection !== null;
   113	}
   114	
   115	export function getEvolverRoot(directory: string): string {
   116		return `${directory}/.evomap`;
   117	}
   118	
   119	export function getMemoryGraphPath(evolverRoot: string): string {
   120		return `${evolverRoot}/memory/evolution/memory_graph.jsonl`;
   121	}

/usr/bin/zsh -lc "nl -ba src/doctor.ts | sed -n '1,280p'" in /home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge
 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	import { access, mkdir, rm, writeFile } from "node:fs/promises";
     2	import path from "node:path";
     3	import { readMemoryGraph } from "./bridge.ts";
     4	import { defaultConfig } from "./config.ts";
     5	import {
     6		detectEvolver,
     7		getEvolverRoot,
     8		getMemoryGraphPath,
     9	} from "./spawn.ts";
    10	
    11	export interface DoctorCheck {
    12		name: string;
    13		status: "pass" | "fail" | "warn";
    14		message: string;
    15		detail?: string;
    16	}
    17	
    18	export interface DoctorResult {
    19		checks: DoctorCheck[];
    20		healthy: boolean;
    21		summary: string;
    22	}
    23	
    24	async function checkEvolverCli(): Promise<DoctorCheck> {
    25		const detection = await detectEvolver();
    26		if (detection) {
    27			return {
    28				name: "Evolver CLI Detection",
    29				status: "pass",
    30				message: `evolver v${detection.version} found at ${detection.path}`,
    31			};
    32		}
    33		return {
    34			name: "Evolver CLI Detection",
    35			status: "fail",
    36			message: "evolver CLI not found. Install with: npm install -g @evomap/evolver",
    37		};
    38	}
    39	
    40	async function checkEvolverRoot(directory: string): Promise<DoctorCheck> {
    41		const evolverRoot = getEvolverRoot(directory);
    42		try {
    43			await access(evolverRoot);
    44			return {
    45				name: "Evolver Root Directory",
    46				status: "pass",
    47				message: ".evomap/ directory exists",
    48				detail: evolverRoot,
    49			};
    50		} catch {
    51			return {
    52				name: "Evolver Root Directory",
    53				status: "warn",
    54				message: ".evomap/ directory not found (will be created on first use)",
    55				detail: evolverRoot,
    56			};
    57		}
    58	}
    59	
    60	async function verifyWriteAccess(filePath: string): Promise<boolean> {
    61		const dir = path.dirname(filePath);
    62		const testPath = path.join(dir, ".doctor-write-test");
    63		await mkdir(dir, { recursive: true });
    64		await writeFile(testPath, "test", "utf8");
    65		await rm(testPath);
    66		return true;
    67	}
    68	
    69	async function checkMemoryGraph(directory: string): Promise<DoctorCheck> {
    70		const evolverRoot = getEvolverRoot(directory);
    71		const graphPath = getMemoryGraphPath(evolverRoot);
    72		const entries = await readMemoryGraph(graphPath);
    73	
    74		if (entries.length > 0) {
    75			try {
    76				await verifyWriteAccess(graphPath);
    77				return {
    78					name: "Memory Graph Access",
    79					status: "pass",
    80					message: `memory_graph.jsonl accessible (${entries.length} entries)`,
    81					detail: graphPath,
    82				};
    83			} catch (err) {
    84				return {
    85					name: "Memory Graph Access",
    86					status: "fail",
    87					message: `Cannot write to memory_graph.jsonl: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`,
    88					detail: graphPath,
    89				};
    90			}
    91		}
    92	
    93		try {
    94			await access(graphPath);
    95			return {
    96				name: "Memory Graph Access",
    97				status: "pass",
    98				message: "memory_graph.jsonl accessible (0 entries)",
    99				detail: graphPath,
   100			};
   101		} catch {
   102			// fallthrough
   103		}
   104	
   105		try {
   106			await mkdir(path.dirname(graphPath), { recursive: true });
   107			await writeFile(graphPath, "", "utf8");
   108			await rm(graphPath);
   109			return {
   110				name: "Memory Graph Access",
   111				status: "warn",
   112				message: "memory_graph.jsonl not found (will be created on first use)",
   113				detail: graphPath,
   114			};
   115		} catch (err) {
   116			return {
   117				name: "Memory Graph Access",
   118				status: "fail",
   119				message: `Cannot write to memory_graph.jsonl: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err)}`,
   120				detail: graphPath,
   121			};
   122		}
   123	}
   124	
   125	async function checkPluginRegistration(directory: string): Promise<DoctorCheck> {
   126		const localPluginPath = path.join(directory, ".opencode", "plugin", "evomap.ts");
   127		const npmPackagePath = path.join(
   128			directory,
   129			"node_modules",
   130			"opencode-evomap-bridge",
   131			"package.json",
   132		);
   133		const npmPluginPath = path.join(
   134			directory,
   135			"node_modules",
   136			"opencode-evomap-bridge",
   137			".opencode",
   138			"plugin",
   139			"evomap.ts",
   140		);
   141	
   142		try {
   143			await access(localPluginPath);
   144			return {
   145				name: "Plugin Registration",
   146				status: "pass",
   147				message: "Plugin file exists at .opencode/plugin/evomap.ts",
   148				detail: localPluginPath,
   149			};
   150		} catch {
   151			// try npm installation mode next
   152		}
   153	
   154		try {
   155			await Promise.all([access(npmPackagePath), access(npmPluginPath)]);
   156			return {
   157				name: "Plugin Registration",
   158				status: "pass",
   159				message: "Plugin package exists in node_modules/opencode-evomap-bridge",
   160				detail: npmPluginPath,
   161			};
   162		} catch {
   163			return {
   164				name: "Plugin Registration",
   165				status: "fail",
   166				message: "Plugin not found in local .opencode path or npm installation",
   167				detail: `Expected one of: ${localPluginPath} OR ${npmPluginPath}`,
   168			};
   169		}
   170	}
   171	
   172	function checkConfiguration(): DoctorCheck {
   173		const config = defaultConfig;
   174	
   175		if (!config.evolverFallbackToLocal) {
   176			return {
   177				name: "Configuration Check",
   178				status: "warn",
   179				message: "evolverFallbackToLocal is false — plugin will produce no observations if evolver is unavailable",
   180				detail: `evolverBinary=${config.evolverBinary}, timeout=${config.evolverSpawnTimeoutMs}ms, fallback=${config.evolverFallbackToLocal}`,
   181			};
   182		}
   183	
   184		return {
   185			name: "Configuration Check",
   186			status: "pass",
   187			message: `Configuration valid (evolverBinary=${config.evolverBinary}, timeout=${config.evolverSpawnTimeoutMs}ms, fallback=${config.evolverFallbackToLocal})`,
   188		};
   189	}
   190	
   191	export async function runDoctor(directory: string): Promise<DoctorResult> {
   192		console.warn("[EvoMapBridge/doctor] Running diagnostics...");
   193	
   194		const checks: DoctorCheck[] = [];
   195	
   196		checks.push(await checkEvolverCli());
   197		checks.push(await checkEvolverRoot(directory));
   198		checks.push(await checkMemoryGraph(directory));
   199		checks.push(await checkPluginRegistration(directory));
   200		checks.push(checkConfiguration());
   201	
   202		const allPass = checks.every((c) => c.status === "pass");
   203		const failCount = checks.filter((c) => c.status === "fail").length;
   204		const warnCount = checks.filter((c) => c.status === "warn").length;
   205	
   206		let summary: string;
   207		if (allPass) {
   208			summary = "All checks passed";
   209		} else {
   210			const parts: string[] = [];
   211			if (failCount > 0) {
   212				parts.push(`${failCount} failed`);
   213			}
   214			if (warnCount > 0) {
   215				parts.push(`${warnCount} warning${warnCount > 1 ? "s" : ""}`);
   216			}
   217			summary = parts.join(", ");
   218		}
   219	
   220		console.warn(`[EvoMapBridge/doctor] ${summary}`);
   221	
   222		return {
   223			checks,
   224			healthy: allPass,
   225			summary,
   226		};
   227	}
   228	
   229	export function formatDoctorResult(result: DoctorResult): string {
   230		const lines: string[] = [];
   231		const statusIcon: Record<string, string> = {
   232			pass: "✓",
   233			fail: "✗",
   234			warn: "⚠",
   235		};
   236	
   237		lines.push("=== EvoMap Bridge Doctor ===");
   238		lines.push("");
   239	
   240		for (const check of result.checks) {
   241			const icon = statusIcon[check.status] ?? "?";
   242			lines.push(`  ${icon} ${check.name}: ${check.message}`);
   243			if (check.detail) {
   244				lines.push(`    → ${check.detail}`);
   245			}
   246		}
   247	
   248		lines.push("");
   249		lines.push(`Summary: ${result.summary}`);
   250	
   251		return lines.join("\n");
   252	}

codex

    17			result: {
    18				success: overrides.result?.success ?? false,
    19				exitCode: overrides.result?.exitCode ?? 1,
    20				durationMs: overrides.result?.durationMs ?? 100,
    21				outputDigest: overrides.result?.outputDigest ?? "digest-1",
    22				errorSnippet: overrides.result?.errorSnippet ?? "Command failed",
    23			},
    24		};
    25	}
    26	
    27	describe("deriveObservations", () => {
    28		test("emits repeat failure after threshold", () => {
    29			const signal = makeSignal({});
    30			const recentSignals = [makeSignal({ id: "a" }), makeSignal({ id: "b" }), signal];
    31			const observations = deriveObservations(signal, recentSignals, defaultConfig);
    32			expect(observations.some((item) => item.type === "repeat_failure")).toBe(true);
    33		});
    34	
    35		test("emits slow execution for long-running tools", () => {
    36			const signal = makeSignal({
    37				result: {
    38					success: true,
    39					exitCode: 0,
    40					durationMs: defaultConfig.slowExecutionMs + 1,
    41					outputDigest: "slow",
    42					errorSnippet: "",
    43				},
    44			});
    45			const observations = deriveObservations(signal, [signal], defaultConfig);
    46			expect(observations.some((item) => item.type === "slow_execution")).toBe(true);
    47		});
    48	});
    49	
    50	describe("renderAdvisories", () => {
    51		test("renders a sentinel-wrapped advisory block", () => {
    52			const rendered = renderAdvisories([
    53				{
    54					id: "adv-1",
    55					tool: "bash",
    56					message: "Avoid repeating the same failing bash command.",
    57					observationId: "obs-1",
    58					createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    59					lastUsedAt: null,
    60					useCount: 0,
    61					maxUses: 3,
    62					cooldownUntil: null,
    63					pathHints: [],
    64					source: "session",
    65				},
    66			]);
    67	
    68			expect(rendered).toContain("<!-- evomap-bridge:advisory -->");
    69			expect(rendered).toContain("Avoid repeating the same failing bash command.");
    70		});
    71	});

codex
不算完整。现在更准确的判断是：`evomap` 的基础闭环已经有了，但离“流程完整、可稳定依赖”还差几处关键环节。

**主要问题**
1. `memory_graph` 的实际数据结构和代码假设不一致，`evolver` 主链路大概率会静默退回本地规则。[src/bridge.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/bridge.ts:58) 假设每条记录都有顶层 `signals`、`timestamp`、`gene_id`；但仓库里的真实数据是 `MemoryGraphEvent`，字段是 `ts`、`kind`，且信号嵌在 `signal.signals` 里，[memory_graph.jsonl](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/memory/evolution/memory_graph.jsonl:1) 和 [memory_graph.jsonl](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/memory/evolution/memory_graph.jsonl:4) 都能看到。这样 `evolverEntryToObservation()` 里的 `entry.signals.map(...)` 会失配，[src/bridge.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/bridge.ts:58)。结果不是“evolver 观察被稳定读回”，而是经常落到 fallback。

2. `session.created` 并没有真正“注入进化记忆”，只是读完后打印 `console.warn`。[.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts:247) 到 [evomap.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts:275)。README 写的是“注入进化记忆”与 session 生命周期闭环，[README.md](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/README.md:13) 和 [README.md](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/README.md:28)，但实现上真正把记忆放进模型上下文的是 `experimental.chat.system.transform`，[.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts:330)。这说明文档里的流程描述比代码更完整。

3. 配置项 `evolverBinary` 目前是“文档存在、运行时无效”。配置里定义了它，[src/config.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/config.ts:16)；README 也暴露了它，[README.md](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/README.md:112)；但检测和执行都硬编码成 `"evolver"`，[src/spawn.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/spawn.ts:13)、[spawn.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/spawn.ts:25)、[spawn.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/spawn.ts:60)。这会让可配置的执行链路名义上存在，实际上不可用。

4. repo 级提升流程只停在 `repoCandidates` 状态里，没有后续审核/落盘/回灌闭环。[src/state.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/state.ts:112) 到 [state.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/src/state.ts:120)。README 也承认“不做 repo 级自动规则落盘”，[README.md](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/README.md:211)。如果你问的是“完整产品流程”，这里显然还没完成。

5. 测试覆盖的是模块级逻辑，不是插件级端到端流程。当前测试没有覆盖 `EvoMapBridgePlugin` 的 hooks、真实 `evolver` 输出格式，也没有覆盖 `session.created/session.idle/system.transform/compacting` 的联动；`evolver` 安装相关测试还是 skip。[tests/evolver.test.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/tests/evolver.test.ts:27) 和测试输出里也能看到 2 个 skip。

**结论**
当前状态可以说是“核心 MVP 已打通”：
`tool.execute.after -> queue -> deriveObservationsWithEvolver/fallback -> state -> tool.execute.before -> advisory`
这条链路是有的，[.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts:150) 到 [evomap.ts](/home/xiaxia/Workspaces/Projects/opencode-evomap-bridge/.opencode/plugin/evomap.ts:244)。

但如果标准是“evomap 流程完整”，我的判断是否定的。最关键的缺口是 `memory_graph` schema 兼容、`session.created` 的真实注入行为，以及 repo 级闭环没完成。

`bun run test` 通过，结果是 `26 pass / 2 skip / 0 fail`；`bun run typecheck` 也通过。  
如果你要，我下一步可以直接把这三个缺口补成真正的闭环。
